### BREAKING CHANGES

* ğŸ§¨ No longer requires react-router as a routing system.
* ğŸ§¨ Button as a link requires LinkProvider
* ğŸ§¨ Link needs a provided react-router link to work as before
* ğŸ§¨ TabNavs requires a custom Link to LinkProvider if to be used with
react-router.
* ğŸ§¨ Dropping support for automatic active with react-router

### BREAKING CHANGES

- ğŸ§¨ flexbox now is a single component, with `container` and `item` as props
- ğŸ§¨ initialActiveId is now correctly initialActiveIndex on Tabs.
- ğŸ§¨ All spinners now require a unique `id` prop.
- ğŸ§¨ `Currency` and `Percent` components are now part of the `Number`
  component. Migrate like so: `<Currency value={100} currency="SEK" />` => `<Number value={100} currency="SEK" />` and `<Percent value={100} />` => `<Number value={100} percentage />`.

- feat: add development component that wraps the number component
- ğŸ§¨`Development` component now behaves as a wrapper around number that adds styling for color, etc.
- ğŸ§¨ remove default styles from CardWithTitle

- test: ğŸ’ update snapshots
- ğŸ§¨ remove padding from cardwithtitle

feat: tabs

- test: updated snapshots
- ğŸ§¨ Development.Primary is removed as well as Currency.Primary and other
  types of this components. From now on wrap everythign font-related in
  <Typography></Typography> component
- ğŸ§¨ remove text input, split Grid into two, remove placeholder
